| <span data-ttu-id="4cdde-952">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4cdde-952">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4cdde-953">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4cdde-953">Value</span></span> |
|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
